# Slicer resources in Chinese

**Topic ID**: 2077
**Date**: 2018-02-13
**URL**: https://discourse.slicer.org/t/slicer-resources-in-chinese/2077

---

## Post #1 by @pieper (2018-02-13 12:53 UTC)

<p>There’s a great set of materials from the WeChat 3D Slicer group in China that are worth looking at:</p>
<p><a href="https://www.slicer.org/wiki/Documentation/Nightly/Training#Resources_for_Chinese_users" class="onebox" target="_blank">https://www.slicer.org/wiki/Documentation/Nightly/Training#Resources_for_Chinese_users</a></p>
<p>They are very well illustrated and for non-Chinese speakers Chrome / Google Translate does a reasonable job of translating the text content.</p>

---

## Post #6 by @leochan2009 (2018-02-19 01:45 UTC)

<p>Hi Dr. Li,</p>
<p>“Pivot Calibration” means 枢轴校准, here is a paper about the technique detail:<br>
<a href="http://yanivresearch.info/writtenMaterial/pivotCalib-SPIE2015.pdf" class="onebox" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">http://yanivresearch.info/writtenMaterial/pivotCalib-SPIE2015.pdf</a></p>
<p>Best,<br>
Longquan</p>

## Post #14 by @lassoan (2020-04-24 13:04 UTC)

<p>Thank you <a class="mention" href="/u/cyufu">@cyufu</a> for these useful resources. We have forum members from more than 100 countries, but most of us only speak a few languages. Since a post is written once and read by up to a few thousand people, it is essential that the post’s <em>writer</em> provides the English translation (automatic translation is OK), as one minute of extra work from the writer saves tens of hours for <em>readers</em>. You can include the original language text as section that can be opened by clicking on it, for example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-auto">[details="Original in Chinese"]
You can write the original text here...
[/details]
</code></pre>
<p>It shows up like this:</p>
<details>
<summary>
Original in Chinese</summary>
<p>You can write the original text here…</p>
</details>

---

## Post #15 by @agirault (2020-04-24 22:05 UTC)

<p>FYI for automated translations, I recommend <a href="https://www.deepl.com/en/translator" rel="noopener nofollow ugc">DeepL</a>.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>参考一下 <a class="mention" href="/u/cyufu">@cyufu</a>，对于自动翻译，我推荐 <a href="https://www.deepl.com/en/translator" rel="noopener nofollow ugc">DeepL</a>。</p>
</blockquote>
